relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="pipes-api-copy-pipes-service" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Pipes API Copy Pipes service<a class="headerlink" href="#pipes-api-copy-pipes-service" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><article><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The API host in the following examples must match your Workspace&#x27;s region. See the full list of <a href="/docs/api-reference#regions-and-endpoints">regions and hosts</a></p></div></div></article><article><p>The Pipes API helps you interact with your Pipes. Several services are included under Pipes:</p><ul><li><a href="#pipes">Pipes</a>: List, create, update, or delete your Tinybird Pipes.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/api-endpoints">API Endpoints</a>: Publish or unpublish your Pipes as API Endpoints.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/materialized-views">Materialized Views and Populates</a>: Create, delete, or populate Materialized Views.</li><li><a href="/docs/api-reference/pipe-api/copy-pipes-api">Scheduled Copy (Copy Pipes API)</a>: Create, delete, schedule, and trigger Copy jobs.</li></ul></article><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-caution text-[#856100]"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.333 10.216a.666.666 0 1 0 0 1.332.666.666 0 0 0 0-1.332m7.114.98L10.08 1.862a2 2 0 0 0-3.493 0l-5.334 9.334a2 2 0 0 0 1.707 3.02h10.747a2 2 0 0 0 1.74-3.02m-1.154 1.333a.67.67 0 0 1-.586.34H2.96a.67.67 0 0 1-.587-.34.67.67 0 0 1 0-.667L7.707 2.53a.667.667 0 0 1 1.186 0l5.367 9.333a.67.67 0 0 1 .033.68zm-5.96-7.647a.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v2.667a.667.667 0 1 0 1.333 0V5.549a.667.667 0 0 0-.667-.667"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Adding or modifying pipes or data sources in <a href="/docs/forward/install-tinybird/local">Tinybird Local</a> and <a href="/docs/forward">Tinybird Forward</a> can only be done through deployments.</p></div></div><h2 id="copy-pipes-api" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Copy Pipes API<a class="headerlink" href="#copy-pipes-api" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The Copy Pipes API helps you create, delete, schedule and trigger <a href="/docs/work-with-data/process-and-copy/copy-pipes">Copy Pipes</a>.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-x-auto"><div class="body" role="main">
            
  <dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes/(.+)/copy</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Calling this endpoint sets the pipe as a Copy one with the given settings. Scheduling is optional.</p>
<p>To run the actual copy after you set the pipe as a Copy one, you must call the POST <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/:pipe/copy</span></code> endpoint.</p>
<p>If you need to change the target Data Source or the scheduling configuration, you can call PUT endpoint.</p>
<p>Restrictions:</p>
<ul class="simple">
<li><p>You can set only one schedule per Copy pipe.</p></li>
<li><p>You can’t set a Copy pipe if the pipe is already materializing. You must unlink the Materialization first.</p></li>
<li><p>You can’t set a Copy pipe if the pipe is already an endpoint. You must unpublish the endpoint first.</p></li>
</ul>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id1">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Setting the pipe as a Copy pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id1" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE and DATASOURCE:APPEND token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/nodes/:node/copy&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;target_datasource=my_destination_datasource&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;schedule_cron=*/15 * * * *&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id2">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id2" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:CREATE</span></code> and <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DATASOURCE:APPEND</span></code> scopes on it</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>target_datasource</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Name or the id of the target Data Source.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>schedule_cron</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. A crontab expression.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id3">

<div class="highlight-json notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">&quot;updated_at&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;2023-03-01 10:34:19.113518&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>

<dl class="http delete">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="delete--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">DELETE</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes/(.+)/copy</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#delete--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Removes the Copy type of the pipe.
By removing the Copy type, nor the node nor the pipe are deleted.
The pipe will still be present, but will stop any scheduled and copy settings.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id4">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Unsetting the pipe as a Copy pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id4" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>DELETE<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/nodes/:node/copy&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id5">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Response codes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id5" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Code</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>204</p></td>
<td><p>No error</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>Wrong node id</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Forbidden. Provided token doesn’t have permissions to publish a pipe, it needs <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">ADMIN</span></code> or <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:CREATE</span></code></p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>404</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe not found</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</dd></dl>

<dl class="http put">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="put--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">PUT</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/nodes/(.+)/copy</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#put--v0-pipes-(.+)-nodes-(.+)-copy" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Calling this endpoint will update a Copy pipe with the given settings: you can change its target Data Source, as well as adding or modifying its schedule.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id6">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Updating a Copy Pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id6" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>PUT<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/nodes/:node/copy&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;target_datasource=other_destination_datasource&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-d<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;schedule_cron=*/15 * * * *&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id7">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id7" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:CREATE</span></code> scope on it</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>target_datasource</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. Name or the id of the target Data Source.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>schedule_cron</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. A crontab expression. If schedule_cron=’None’ the schedule will be removed from the copy pipe, if it was defined</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>mode</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The mode to use for the copy pipe. Can be ‘append’ or ‘replace’. Default is ‘append’.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/copy</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Runs a copy job, using the settings previously set in the pipe.
You can use this URL to do an on-demand copy.
This URL is also used by the scheduler to make the programmed calls.</p>
<p>This URL accepts parameters, just like in a regular endpoint.</p>
<p>This operation is asynchronous and will copy the output of the endpoint to an existing datasource.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id9">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Runs a copy job on a Copy pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id9" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl
<span class="w">    </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:READ token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">    </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/copy?param1=test&amp;param2=test2&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id10">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Request parameters</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id10" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 60.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Key</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Type</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>token</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Auth token. Ensure it has the <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:READ</span></code> scope on it</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>parameters</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. The value of the parameters to run the Copy with. They are regular URL query parameters.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>_mode</p></td>
<td><p>String</p></td>
<td><p>Optional. One of ‘append’ or ‘replace’. Default is ‘append’.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table class="docutils align-default" id="id11">
<caption><span class="caption-text">Response codes</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id11" title="Permalink to this table">¶</a></caption>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20.0%" >
<col style="width: 80.0%" >
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr class="row-odd"><th class="head"><p>Code</p></th>
<th class="head"><p>Description</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>200</p></td>
<td><p>No error</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe is not a Copy pipe or there is a problem with the SQL query</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>400</p></td>
<td><p>The columns in the SQL query don’t match the columns in the target Data Source</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Forbidden. The provided token doesn’t have permissions to append a node to the pipe (<code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">ADMIN</span></code> or <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">PIPE:READ</span></code> and <code class="docutils literal notranslate"><span class="pre">DATASOURCE:APPEND</span></code>)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even"><td><p>403</p></td>
<td><p>Job limits exceeded. Tried to copy more than 100M rows, or there are too many active (working and waiting) Copy jobs.</p></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd"><td><p>404</p></td>
<td><p>Pipe not found, Node not found or Target Data Source not found</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>The response will not be the final result of the copy but a Job. You can check the job status and progress using the <a class="reference external" href="/docs/api-reference/jobs-api">Jobs API</a>.</p>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-pause">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/copy/pause</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-pause" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Pauses the scheduling. This affects any future scheduled Copy job. Any copy operation currently copying data will be completed.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id13">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Pauses a scheduled copy</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id13" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">        </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">       </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/copy/pause&quot;</span>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-resume">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/copy/resume</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-resume" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Resumes a previously paused scheduled copy.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id15">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Resumes a Scheduled copy</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id15" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">        </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>

<dl class="http post">
<dt class="sig sig-object http" id="post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-cancel">
<span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">POST</span> </span><span class="sig-name descname"><span class="pre">/v0/pipes/(.+)/copy/cancel</span></span><a class="headerlink" href="#post--v0-pipes-(.+)-copy-cancel" title="Permalink to this definition">¶</a></dt>
<dd><p>Cancels jobs that are working or waiting that are tied to the pipe and pauses the scheduling of copy jobs for this pipe.
To allow scheduled copy jobs to run for the pipe, the copy pipe must be resumed and the already cancelled jobs will not be resumed.</p>
<div class="literal-block-wrapper docutils container" id="id17">
<div class="code-block-caption"><span class="caption-text">Cancels scheduled copy jobs tied to the pipe</span><a class="headerlink" href="#id17" title="Permalink to this code">¶</a></div>
<div class="highlight-bash notranslate"><div class="highlight"><pre><span></span>curl<span class="w"> </span>-X<span class="w"> </span>POST<span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">        </span>-H<span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">&quot;Authorization: Bearer &lt;PIPE:CREATE token&gt;&quot;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="se">\</span>
<span class="w">       </span><span class="s2">&quot;<span data-user-custom="apiHost">https://&lt;your_host&gt;</span>/v0/pipes/:pipe/copy/cancel&quot;</span>
</pre></div>
</div>
</div>
